<script>
  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_b66665e3-d458-43a0-9c5a-8d7f0281b6f1'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

<div id="descriptionContainer">
  
      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer11267979877012474428"><i>Librarian Note: Alternate Cover Edition for <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17981514-don-t-make-me-beautiful' rel='nofollow noopener'>ASIN: B00EZ5R78O</a>.</i><br/><br/><b><i>NEW YORK TIMES</i> and <i>USA TODAY</i> BESTSELLING AUTHOR, ELLE CASEY, brings readers the romantic suspense novel DON’T MAKE ME BEAUTIFUL.</b><br/><br/><i>This story was inspired by true events. If you liked the movie "Sleeping With the Enemy", then you might like this story too.</i> <br/><br/>No one knew a woman lived there or that she even existed. A </span>
  <span id="freeText11267979877012474428" style="display:none"><i>Librarian Note: Alternate Cover Edition for <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17981514-don-t-make-me-beautiful" rel="nofollow noopener">ASIN: B00EZ5R78O</a>.</i><br /><br /><b><i>NEW YORK TIMES</i> and <i>USA TODAY</i> BESTSELLING AUTHOR, ELLE CASEY, brings readers the romantic suspense novel DON’T MAKE ME BEAUTIFUL.</b><br /><br /><i>This story was inspired by true events. If you liked the movie "Sleeping With the Enemy", then you might like this story too.</i> <br /><br />No one knew a woman lived there or that she even existed. A monster, living in darkness...<br /><br />At twenty-two, Nicole doesn't even look human anymore. The beast made sure of that. So she hides. A monster, consigned to a life of fear and solitude. This is all she deserves, she is quite sure of that.  And then one day out of the blue, the autographed baseball caught by Brian Jensen at the latest Marlins game enters her prison and manages to turn her world completely upside down.<br /><br />Temptation comes in the form of pity at first, and then perhaps something more. Does she dare to believe the things she's told, that this is not the life she was meant to live? That being a monster is not her forever-fate? And will she be willing to risk everything, to reach out and accept the helping hands around her and share her deepest, darkest secrets? She knows only too well that hands can hurt. Finding out whether they can also heal is a risky proposition, especially when the beast is still out there. Looking for her.<br /><br /><i>Content warning: Violence, foul language, and adult situations. Not meant for younger readers.</i> <br /><br /><b>A note from Elle about this book:</b> A really long time ago, I read an article in a newspaper or a magazine (I haven’t been able to locate the original) about a woman who was so badly beaten over a long period of time, she couldn’t leave her house. I thought about that woman a lot over the years and about what her thoughts might have been, her fears, her reality … and this book was my attempt to both exorcise those thoughts from my brain and also shed some light on a subject —domestic violence— that I feel should never be left in darkness.</span>
  <a data-text-id="11267979877012474428" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      </div>
</div>

<div id="bookReviews">
  




  <div class="friendReviews elementListBrown" >
    <div class="section firstReview">
      

<div id="review_716496386" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/716496386" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/716496386?book_show_action=true">Sep 10, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer716496386" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14830984463389088599"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380436205i/881582._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>First, here's my casting for Brian:<br/><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380436205i/881583._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>*** FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED ***<br/><br/>WOW!! I absolutely loved this book!!! 5 stars! <br/><br/><strong><em>Don't Make Me Beautiful</em> is a deeply touching, beautiful and inspiring story with a powerful message about the strength of survival and the healing power of love. <br/><br/>It's both heart breaking and heart warming with a strong heroine, a to-die-for hero, and a story that will stay with you long after you finish reading. It touched my heart deeply and reminded me that there are still superheroe</strong></span>
  <span id="freeText14830984463389088599" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380436205i/881582._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>First, here's my casting for Brian:<br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380436205i/881583._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>*** FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED ***<br><br>WOW!! I absolutely loved this book!!! 5 stars! <br><br><strong><em>Don't Make Me Beautiful</em> is a deeply touching, beautiful and inspiring story with a powerful message about the strength of survival and the healing power of love. <br><br>It's both heart breaking and heart warming with a strong heroine, a to-die-for hero, and a story that will stay with you long after you finish reading. It touched my heart deeply and reminded me that there are still superheroes out there everyday who save each other. <br><br>This is easily one of my favorites of the year! </strong><br><br>I first fell in love with Elle Casey's writing with her witty romantic comedy, <em>Shine Not Burn, </em>and when I learned that she'd released a new, more serious romance, I couldn't wait to try out another side of her writing and let me tell you -- I was blown away!!<br><br>The story is that of a brutally abused woman, Nicole, whose face has been horribly disfigured after years of beatings at the hands of a man she once thought she loved. She was conditioned to never escape and her body had been broken and rebroken more times than she could count.<br><br>Brian is a single dad whose whole world revolves around his son. Things may not have worked out with his ex-wife but they remained good friends and his focus is on living in the moment and hoping that maybe one day, if it's mean to be, the right person will come along who can complete his family.<br><br>When fate crosses his paths with Nicole's, he rescues her, takes her to the hospital under a fake name and offers to take her home with him to give her a safe place to heal. He might not know anything about her but he wants to help shelter her and help her give her back the life that was stolen from her.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>“I’m no superhero.”</em>
    <br>
    <em>“Tell that to the girl you’re rescuing.”</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>Ok, first of all, despite the fact that this book might seem dark, it's really not. The base subject matter is grim but I generally found the story to be very heart warming. Because this is inspired by true events, it restored some of my faith in humanity and reminded me that there are true super heroes out there living among us each day.<br><br>I was hooked from the first chapter. I <em>felt</em> Nicole's pain, isolation and desperation. Seeing how happy she used to be and how broken she was now was gut wrenching and I knew I wanted to see her journey to safety and happiness.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"If only she'd known then what she knows now, she would have picked up the nearest weapon and beat John to death the minute she met him. Instead she dated him, moved in with him, and then became his prisoner."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>The things she suffered at the hands of her boyfriend/abuser were sickening. There were no graphic descriptions but just the thought of any human being going through that made my stomach turn. I think a huge part of what added to how chilling it was though was the fact that this was all happening in a normal house in the middle of a suburban neighbourhood. It wasn't some creepy shack in the middle of nowhere. This was right in plain sight. <em>And nobody noticed!!</em><br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"She gave up somewhere along the way out of a sense of survival."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>Brian, was just absolutely to-die-for <em>amazing</em>!!! He honestly might be one of the most heroic and truly <em>incredible</em> people I've ever read about. A true 
  <em>hero</em>
 in every sense of the word. He was the embodiment of kind, caring and protective. He was a wonderful dad, a supportive ex-husband, and just generally the kind of person who just made you feel safe.<br><br>When he <em>found</em> her, I just felt such strong relief. He rescued her, saved her, sheltered her and helped her heal. He went above and beyond because that's just what was in his nature. The world would be a better place with more Brians in it.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"Why would you do that for me? I'm just a woman with a destroyed face and body and no where to go?" …</em>
    <br>
    <br>
    <em>"No, you're not. You're a girl who fell in love with the wrong guy. Your face doesn't matter, it's your heart that's important. And if you can love a guy like that, then I know it has to be twice the size of a normal one. Beside… you do have somewhere to go. You're going to my place now... you had a few years of your life taken away from you. Now we're going to get them back… You're going to stumble, but that's what I'm here for. Lean on me. I'll keep you from falling."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>She was scared, terrified even, that her abuser/boyfriend would find her and her instinct told her to run back and avoid the trauma of him finding her after she'd escaped. But Brian would hear none of it. He could see the strong girl hidden behind the scars and was determined to bring back that side of her.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"I need to go back."<br><br></em>
    <em>"Bullshit… You are NOT going back there. I don't care what you say… I'm not letting you go back."<br><br></em>
    <em>"You're not my keeper." …<br><br></em>
    <em>"You are your own keeper, Nicole. I'm just your protector."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>That just made me melt. I love that he saw right past her scars. He saw <em>her - </em>the girl underneath it all and was drawn to her. Remember that this <em>is</em> a romance but, given Nicole's situation and everything she'd been through, that side of the story understandably was slow building for the first while allowing time for healing first. I really enjoyed the pacing and loved that it was never rushed and that they bonded first as friends before anything.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"Scars are your body's way of healing, making that damaged part stronger than it ever was before the pain." </em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>The more he made her feel comfortable, the more the <em>real</em> her emerged. She was such a fun girl! Full of life, a little snark and had the biggest heart. They really were a perfect match and if anyone deserved a knight in shining armour, it truly was her.<br><br>But this wasn't just about healing, this was also about a woman taking charge of her life once again after it had been stolen from her. <em>Owning</em> her life once again. Facing her demons. Seeing the strength that Brian helped her find again and then the rest of the strength that she found on her own was truly inspiring.<br><br>This might sound odd to say because it so rarely happens in books but I actually also really loved the relationship that Brian had with his ex-wife. They truly were best friends. They loved each dearly but weren't <i>in love </i>with each other. It was so nice to see a divorced couple in a book who weren't at each other's throats and who genuinely supported each other and wanted each other to be happy.<br><br>In fact, every single one of the supporting characters was wonderful -- especially Helen (the ex-wife), Agnes (the next-door neighbour) and Liam (Brian's adorable son). I fell in love with them all in their own way. Except of course John, the abusive monster who, as Helen said, "<em>deserves to be butt raped in jail</em>."<br><br>Another thing that I really loved about this book was that I absolutely respected and understood every decision each character made. Never once did I roll my eyes or want to shake anyone. I'm always very impressed when a book comes a long like this this where I can genuinely respect each one of the characters and where the drama comes from completely external sources. To me that speaks volumes for the strength of the story itself that it's able to be <em>this</em> captivating without any unnecessary drama.<br><br>There was a twist in the last 20% or so that sent full body <em>shivers</em> through me!! I absolutely <em>loved</em> the direction it took the story in and I read the ending with happy tears in my eyes as everything came together. It was truly beautiful and I was left with the most wonderful feeling <em>ever!!!</em><br><br><em>Don't Make Me Beautiful</em> is a beautiful, poignant and unforgettable story about survival, healing, and a second chance at life and love. It made me laugh and cry and feel with my whole heart <strong>❤</strong><br><br>Seriously, someone needs to make this into a movie!!<br><br>Highly recommended!<br><br><b> 5 stars! </b><br><br>PS - this is a standalone.<br><br>****************************<br><br><b> For more of my reviews, book news and updates:<br>✦ <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Main blog: Aestas Book Blog</a><br>✦ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook Blog Page</a><br>✦ <a href="https://twitter.com/AestasBookBlog" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> <br><br><a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380306821i/688100._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="14830984463389088599" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_713573330" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/713573330" />
    <a title="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister"><img alt="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1486056026p2/4971692.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/713573330?book_show_action=true">Sep 06, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" href="/user/show/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister">Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=suspenseful">suspenseful</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=abuse">abuse</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer713573330" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17625704173487616292"><b>*3.5 Stars*</b><br/><br/>While I didn't end up falling in love with the delivery of this story, I respect its content and the brave messages it so strongly conveyed. <br/><br/><i>Don't Make Me Beautiful</i> centers on one woman's escape of an extremely brutal and heartbreaking case of domestic abuse. The beginning presents fairly gruesome events that, although potentially difficult for some to witness, are detrimental in communicating an honest representation of the abuse. <br/><br/><b>Nicole</b> is a woman who is trapped in a physically and </span>
  <span id="freeText17625704173487616292" style="display:none"><b>*3.5 Stars*</b><br><br>While I didn't end up falling in love with the delivery of this story, I respect its content and the brave messages it so strongly conveyed. <br><br><i>Don't Make Me Beautiful</i> centers on one woman's escape of an extremely brutal and heartbreaking case of domestic abuse. The beginning presents fairly gruesome events that, although potentially difficult for some to witness, are detrimental in communicating an honest representation of the abuse. <br><br><b>Nicole</b> is a woman who is trapped in a physically and mentally abusive relationship; one that has not only crippled her integrity but has dramatically deformed her physical appearance to the point where people see her as a "monster"...<br><br>Except people <b>DON'T</b> see her. She has become an unwilling prisoner to the confines of her home, where she is sadly hidden from the world around her. Until a child, a baseball, and a broken window rock the foundation of her tortured world. <br><br><b>Brian</b> is a man with a genuine kindness. When he sees Nicole, it becomes his selfless mission to rescue her from not only her circumstance, but from the unwarranted blame she places on herself. His gentle and understanding, yet firm and persistent persona is exactly what Nicole needs to pull her back to life. <br><br><i>
  <blockquote>
    <b>Listen, you're going to stumble, but that's what I'm here for. Lean on me. I'll keep you from falling.</b>
  </blockquote>
</i><br>There are a few twists and suspenseful turns in this story that do NOT disappoint. The writing is fairly simplistic, but I felt it became a gentle way of presenting such difficult subject matter. Although this story is based on a heartbreaking scenario, I found the majority of it uplifting and was surprised to find much lightheartedness within its pages. The plot could have easily remained dark, but it gracefully placed more emphasis on positive growth rather than becoming swallowed up by the violence. <br><br>What didn't entirely win me over was this story's pace and believability. I felt the hero's portrayal was a bit <i>too</i> flawless and perfect ... consistently doing and saying the all right things ... never once faltering as a parent, a friend, a lover. Yes, it was inspiring, but his character lacked the feel of being "human". That's not to say I needed him to be broken, cruel, or conniving — but for me, his 'superhero' character sometimes felt robotic.<br><br>Although the way everything so perfectly unfolded felt a bit unnatural at times, the family and friendship bonds that formed warmed my heart and made me smile. Yes, this plot resembles <i>Sleeping With the Enemy</i> in the way the heroine runs from an abusive situation, but it's aftermath subtlety displayed the charm and gratification of a fairy tale ... a very unconventional, largely twisted, but happily-ever-after fairy tale — and that's not to make light of the very real and disgusting truths to domestic abuse. I feel this story does a wonderful job in getting across the healthy ways to face and handle such a serious and heartbreaking circumstance, and offers a very lovely and positive message of seeing the beauty within. <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>Love sees inside the person. It doesn't stop at the surface. That stuff is all just window dressing, anyway. It says nothing about what you're really getting. </blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2mh7uop" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="50" width="50" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380347313i/701667.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><b>
  <u>Book Stats:</u>
</b><br><b>▪	 Genre/Category:</b> Romantic Suspense/Abuse<br><b>▪	 Steam Caliber:</b> Moderate<br><b>▪ Romance:</b> Hesitant but sweet and heartwarming. <br><b>▪	 Characters:</b> Strong and sweet hero. Abused and emotionally broken heroine.<br><b>▪	 Plot:</b> a broken woman escaping an abusive and destructive relationship. <br><b>▪ Writing:</b> Raw, vivid.<br><b>▪ POV:</b> 3rd Person Perspective<br><b>▪	 Cliffhanger:</b> None/Standalone<br><br><a href="http://prettywordsbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412050368i/11316768.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/Pretty-Words-Book-Blog/860331017317983" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height='“40"' width="150" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413062455i/11461733._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<div id="review_706486937" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/706486937" />
    <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads"><img alt="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1380942477p2/4197769.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/706486937?book_show_action=true">Aug 29, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads">Jacqueline&#39;s Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=4-star-books">4-star-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=arc">arc</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer706486937" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13534242474371928406"><br/><a href='http://imgur.com/TiqfGf6' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434742i/877815._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>4.5 Stars</b><br/><br/><b>Don’t make me Beautiful is a mixture of <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/537686779' rel='nofollow noopener'>Safe Haven</a> and <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/403008377' rel='nofollow noopener'>Slave</a>. It’s a damsel in distress story line that will grip your heart from start to finish.</b><br/><br/>I loved <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/659722726' rel='nofollow noopener'>Shine Not Burn</a>, so I was very excited for Elle Casey’s newest book, Don’t Make Me Beautiful. Okay, so “Romantic Suspense” isn’t a genre I usually read, BUT it’s an Elle Casey book, so I had to read it. Don’t make me beautiful made me realize how much I do love those deep emotional, you-want-to-give-the-Heroine-a-hug story line. <br/><br/><a href='http://imgur.com/SxHk4Mg' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  </a></span>
  <span id="freeText13534242474371928406" style="display:none"><br><a href="http://imgur.com/TiqfGf6" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434742i/877815._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>4.5 Stars</b><br><br><b>Don’t make me Beautiful is a mixture of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/537686779" rel="nofollow noopener">Safe Haven</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/403008377" rel="nofollow noopener">Slave</a>. It’s a damsel in distress story line that will grip your heart from start to finish.</b><br><br>I loved <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/659722726" rel="nofollow noopener">Shine Not Burn</a>, so I was very excited for Elle Casey’s newest book, Don’t Make Me Beautiful. Okay, so “Romantic Suspense” isn’t a genre I usually read, BUT it’s an Elle Casey book, so I had to read it. Don’t make me beautiful made me realize how much I do love those deep emotional, you-want-to-give-the-Heroine-a-hug story line. <br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/SxHk4Mg" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434742i/877816.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Nicole is in an abusive relationship and for over three years her boyfriend has beaten her to the point where she is not pretty anymore. Her scars and beatings have taken such a toll on her body that she can’t fully recover. She’s trapped in her own home and misery. One day, a little boy hits a ball into her home and breaks a window. The father of the boy is Brian. Brian is just your average guy with an average life, but he soon finds himself in a situation he can’t walk away from.<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/dtLiRel" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434742i/877817.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>I know who I am and I know who he is. He’s no match for me<br><br>You listen to me, you stubborn little thing… you can’t tell me what I think about you, okay? That’s for me to decide.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>WOW, is all I got to say. First off, I love me a damsel in distress story line, so yes to that. Also, there are no flashbacks. I know! How can you write a story about an abused Heroine with no flashbacks? I do not know, but it worked and it was perfect for me. Also, you FELT for Nicole. Oh god, you just want to jump through the pages and just say <b>“GIRL.YOU.ARE.BEAUTIUFL!”</b><br><br>This isn’t really your typical, oh girl gets beat up and guy comes to save her read. I felt like there was a lot that went on and when you add the whole image issue, it just creates another delicious layer. I like Brian, he’s such a sweet man and definitely has the guy-next-door vibe, plus you add in an adorable kid and well it’s a great duo. The relationship between Nicole and Brian progressives gradually and there’s plenty of push back on Nicole’s part to keep you interested in the read.<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/5TRC08y" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434742i/877818.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/AVsCbVW" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434742i/877819.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>It only took five days for her to go from invisible woman living in a house around the corner to the center of his universe</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Despite the subject matter, I wouldn’t call Don’t Make Me Beautiful a difficult book to read and it’s not really steamy. I think in all honesty it’s a beautiful story of moving forward and discovering yourself. I have never been abused, but I know people who have and it’s a very difficult and emotional subject to touch upon. I believe Elle delivered and wrote a beautiful story and it shocked me when I read a note in the book that it was based on true events. You can tell she poured her heart into the writing and it shows.<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/h2QtUGy" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434742i/877820.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Don’t Make Me Beautiful isn’t for everyone. Realize it’s about a women who is traumatized, broken and is coming to terms with her situation, all in the process of a caring man trying to help her through it. If you like that then Don’t Make Me Beautiful is perfect for you.<br><br><i>An ARC was provided in exchange for an honest review</i><br><br>For more reviews, please visit <a href="http://jacquelinesreads.blogspot.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Jacqueline’s Reads</a><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="13534242474371928406" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1687880433" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1687880433" />
    <a title="Dilek VT" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/49572641-dilek-vt"><img alt="Dilek VT" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1448923258p2/49572641.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1687880433?book_show_action=true">Jul 04, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dilek VT" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dilek VT" href="/user/show/49572641-dilek-vt">Dilek VT</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=domestic-violence">domestic-violence</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=disappointing">disappointing</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=abuse">abuse</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1687880433" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17525754345416948748"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1467680584ra/19617263.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>That book hugely disappointed me. Domestic violence is an issue all of us should be sensitive about and when films are made or books are written about it, I appreciate the effort; that is why I read this book but it didn’t make sense at all.<br/><br/>Having grown up in a home where there was domestic violence, I have a pretty good idea what it feels like and many things in this book sounded so wrong to me.<br/><br/><b>Before telling you my problems about this book, let me describe the severe condition of the abused gi</b></span>
  <span id="freeText17525754345416948748" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1467680584ra/19617263.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>That book hugely disappointed me. Domestic violence is an issue all of us should be sensitive about and when films are made or books are written about it, I appreciate the effort; that is why I read this book but it didn’t make sense at all.<br><br>Having grown up in a home where there was domestic violence, I have a pretty good idea what it feels like and many things in this book sounded so wrong to me.<br><br><b>Before telling you my problems about this book, let me describe the severe condition of the abused girl.</b> But from now on, my review may contain spoilers and if you are going to read this book no matter what, then don't read my review.<br><br>There is this girl, Nicole, who chose a wrong person as a boyfriend at the age of 19 and has been abused, both beaten and raped by him in his house where he kept her locked and as a prisoner for three years. <br><br>As a result of years of physical and emotional abuse as well as psychological pressure, her brain is washed and she believes that she has no way to escape. Believing there is no hope for her, she has stopped trying to escape. She doesn’t even try to break a window and cry for help when he is not at home. She has tried only once and when she failed, she never tried again. <br><br>She is beaten continuously and more than 20 bones were broken in her body and because she was never hospitalized, the bones healed themselves irregularly. She has one or two teeth only. And after repeated blows on her face, her nose, jaw and cheekbones also lost their natural shapes. Her ears are damaged, and with her damaged and bent face, she looks like a monster.<br><br>And the sadistic boyfriend keeps a photo of her from the times when she was beautiful and every now and then he forces her to look in the mirror and then at the photo and compare herself with it. Pure torture... <br><br>She also got pregnant and gave the child an early birth after being beaten brutally in the abdomen, and the child died as soon as she was born or so she was told.<br><br><b>So, have you pictured her now?</b><br><br>Well, then, one day, by accident, a neighbor and his 6-year old son discover the existence of this girl and the boy’s father rescues her from that house.<br><br><b>From then on, things started to sound so very wrong to me. </b><br><br>The man who rescued her is a handsome man who is thoughtful, loving and tender. He is willing to help her until she is safe from that evil man. <br><br>This is good...<br>This is good but...<br>But, yes, there is a big but here…<br><br>Her face is described as a monster’s face, so very ugly that when his child first saw her, he ran away in fear. Whoever sees her, they think she looks awful. She needs a series of plastic surgery. <br><br>But this good man, who thinks beauty is inside not outside falls in love with her. And she also finds him very attractive and she falls for him, too. <br><br><b>I just had a hard time to believe this! </b><br><br>If there is going to be some romance in a book like this, you don’t have to start it a week after she was saved from that abusing monster. Even her broken bones are not healed yet, let alone her psychology. Such an insta-love that doesn't feel right or probable here!<br><br>And the sex... Gah! She was continuously beaten and raped by that boyfriend, which requires a serious amount of therapy to heal but this girl falls for him immediately. And after she believes that he really wants her, she literally jumps on him, getting naked in an instant ... sooo eager!!!<br><br>It was neither emotional nor hot for me, I just felt utterly disturbed by the untimely and unrealistic sex scenes in this book.<br><br><b>I am sorry but I cannot accept this as reality. </b><br><br>A week with a handsome and gentle stranger cannot make you heal like that all of a sudden.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1467737588ra/19624632.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>In a situation like this, there are a few things that must be done. </b><br><br>- Letting the police know about it so that the man can be arrested is the first thing you should do. <br>- Then, the woman should first be healed physically and then she should take the necessary amount of therapy. <br>- And meanwhile, she needs people who take care of her, not trying to have sex with her before her broken bones are healed. <br><br><b>Well, did they do all these logical things?<br>NOOOO! Of course, not! </b><br><br>- First of all, she refused to report to the police and they all accepted her decision!<br>- She didn’t want therapy because she didn’t want to talk about the terrifying things she endured and they also accepted it. <br><br><b>WTF?</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1467737423ra/19624616.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Come on, no person with psychological problems go to a therapist cheerfully and willingly, you should make them believe that they seriously need it to heal and to survive. You can’t say, “OK, however you wish”. <br><br>She also wanted to get out of the hospital before she was completely healed and he did as she wished. Come on, take her to a god damn dentist, at least! She doesn't have teeth!<br><br>And if she is afraid that the police will not help her, you should also try to make her see that this is absolute nonsense. <br><br>But no, they don’t report him to the police and <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[the man follows them and of course kidnaps her again!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>Yes, why not? If you are so stupid, this is what would happen!<br><br>Also, this girl looks awful and ugly (this is what the book says, not me) and she needs to have a lot of plastic surgeries to gain her previous appearance back. <br><br><b>Another absurdity happens there! </b><br><br>Minutes before the operation (yes, minutes before the operation), she tells the doctor she doesn’t want to look like the way she did in her photo. She was really a beautiful girl before. And she says she doesn’t want to be beautiful anymore! When the surgeon says he can put her face back to its original shape, she refuses it. <br><br>Her reason is she believes that she had to endure all that abuse because she was beautiful. She believes that her boyfriend got jealous of her because other people also found her beautiful (not because he was a psycho!). So, she doesn’t want to attract any attention anymore! <br><br>So what happens when she says, <b>“Don’t make me beautiful”?</b> The surgeon says, “OK, however you wish” again and he doesn’t make her beautiful!!!<br><br>Come on, she cannot think healthily because she didn’t have therapy so she thinks being beautiful is a curse whereas in reality the reason was the fact that she unfortunately met someone who was a psycho! <br><br>So, in this state of mind, you cannot operate her. You cannot accept her wish as a sane and healthy decision when her wish is so absurd. Let her heal psychologically first and then, ask her again how to do the operation. Psychologically unhealthy people cannot make the right decisions for themselves.<br><br><b>I was totally going insane reading all those pages!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1467737040ra/19624556.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Oh, at the very end of the book, when everything comes to a kind of resolution, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[marriage and child issues all done <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, she decides that she can now start therapy... <br>Oh, really?! <br><br>OK, so I am furious because this book had such good potential with a plot like this but all these absurdities made me go crazy.<br><br>Also, even when there was no absurdity, even the scenes of abuse made me feel nothing because of the way it was written. I should have cried ugly but I didn't feel much, which was strange. Lesser amount of abuse in other books made me cry so hard but here... zero, zilch, zip, nil, nought, nothing... <br><br>I definitely do not recommend this book to anyone. <br><br>My 2 stars are for only dealing with a plot like domestic violence and taking the attention of people to this issue, not anything else.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_958875839" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/958875839" />
    <a title="Beverly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13095060-beverly"><img alt="Beverly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1466964369p2/13095060.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/958875839?book_show_action=true">Jun 05, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beverly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beverly" href="/user/show/13095060-beverly">Beverly</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer958875839" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6121309664249416452"><i>
  <b>Let me start by saying this subject matter, domestic abuse, is very near and dear to my heart. I think it is very serious and my heart goes out to individuals in these situations.</b>
</i><br/><br/>Nicole is living with a monster. For the past three years she has endured endless abuse. The mental abuse has broken her down and made her weak and vulnerable. The physical abuse has made her look like a monster, to the point she scares children. <br/><br/>A lot of people who read this have issues with Nicole staying in an ab</span>
  <span id="freeText6121309664249416452" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>Let me start by saying this subject matter, domestic abuse, is very near and dear to my heart. I think it is very serious and my heart goes out to individuals in these situations.</b>
</i><br /><br />Nicole is living with a monster. For the past three years she has endured endless abuse. The mental abuse has broken her down and made her weak and vulnerable. The physical abuse has made her look like a monster, to the point she scares children. <br /><br />A lot of people who read this have issues with Nicole staying in an abusive relationship for 3 years, or have issues with her refusal to go to the police after the beating that nearly took her life. I am not one of those people. I think it is very realistic, and I feel that it is easy for us women who have never been in that situation to say what we would do.<br /><br />When I started reading this I actually told the girls buddy reading with me, that I loved this story and it could easily become a favorite. My heart broke for Nicole and I loved that Brian was so compassionate towards a stranger. <br /><br />Then at around 35% the story lost me. Here is how I felt. <br /><br /><i>I was traveling down the interstate going 70 mph, on the edge of my seat with excitement. Then all the sudden my car died, and I started coasting. I had to wait until about 60% for things to start back up again. Only to have them slow back down again.</i><br /><br />Honestly, I wish I loved this one, and going in I had high hopes. <br /><br />In the end it fell flat for a few reasons. I didn’t love how the story seemed to slow down to an almost halt, before picking up over 20% later. Once it did pick up again, it didn’t take long for things to level out again. I didn’t love the insta-love connection. I get she is damaged, but it felt like the insta-love was coming more for Brian then Nicole.<br /><br />I enjoyed this story, but didn’t love it. I will say if you do take the time to read it, I recommend finishing it. There were multiple times I was ready to throw in the towel, but I am glad I stuck it out and finished it.</span>
  <a data-text-id="6121309664249416452" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/728217552" />
    <a title="Sarah" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10149843-sarah"><img alt="Sarah" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1593628440p2/10149843.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/728217552?book_show_action=true">Sep 26, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sarah" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sarah" href="/user/show/10149843-sarah">Sarah</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer728217552" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5604841428548946608"><br/><a href='http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/Sarahliteralhottie/media/image_zpsaefee7d9.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384876875i/7007980.jpg' alt=' photo image_zpsaefee7d9.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Don't make me beautiful is the story of Nicole. Nicole is trapped in an abusive relationship, her boyfriend has beaten and tortured her to the point where she no longer recognises herself in the mirror. She can no longer see a way out and has resigned herself to always being trapped, always being a prisoner. She has continuously been broken down and along the way she has lost so much more than just herself........<br/><br/><a href='http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/Sarahliteralhottie/media/image_zps167c20a6.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384876875i/7007981._SX540_.jpg' alt=' photo image_zps167c20a6.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Until one day a little boy hits a ball and breaks her window, and this simp</span>
  <span id="freeText5604841428548946608" style="display:none"><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/Sarahliteralhottie/media/image_zpsaefee7d9.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384876875i/7007980.jpg" alt=" photo image_zpsaefee7d9.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Don't make me beautiful is the story of Nicole. Nicole is trapped in an abusive relationship, her boyfriend has beaten and tortured her to the point where she no longer recognises herself in the mirror. She can no longer see a way out and has resigned herself to always being trapped, always being a prisoner. She has continuously been broken down and along the way she has lost so much more than just herself........<br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/Sarahliteralhottie/media/image_zps167c20a6.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384876875i/7007981._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zps167c20a6.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Until one day a little boy hits a ball and breaks her window, and this simple act brings Brian into her life.<br><br>Now I don't want to give too much more of the story away but what Elle Casey gives the reader in this book isn't simply a story about domestic violence. It's not simply a book about the victim of abuse, it's so much more than that. Elle gives us a beautiful love story about new beginnings, moving forward, learning to trust again and believing that <b>despite the many monsters in this world, there are still some knights in shining armour waiting to catch us when we fall. </b><br><br>This review took me a while to write, it was hard because I didn't know how I could do justice to a book that touches on such a difficult subject matter, yet isn't all doom and gloom and unbearably dark. It was hard because I didn't know how I could explain how very real the author makes the story feel, how her writing flows so effortlessly that she was able to bring Nicole's character to life. <br><br>It was hard because it's a book that gives the reader a very raw insight into the life of a woman who has been beaten and broken both physically and emotionally, over and over again. Yet the author wrote it in a way that turned a heartbreaking story into a story of hope, a story about learning to trust again and moving on after some heartbreaking goodbyes. <br><br>It was a story, the author tells us, which was inspired by true events, about a woman who decides to make a stand, to trust in others and let herself be saved and despite some reviewers feeling it wasn't always a believable story, that surely no victim of abuse would react the way Nicole did.....well for me I never questioned it's believability, for me it was very real, because I was one of the lucky ones, and like Nicole, I was saved by my very own, real life, 'Brian', for whom everyday I am truly thankful. <br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/Sarahliteralhottie/media/image_zps3a80da61.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384876875i/7007982.jpg" alt=" photo image_zps3a80da61.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br></span>

<div id="review_722885454" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/722885454" />
    <a title="K" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16359109-k"><img alt="K" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1357989852p2/16359109.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/722885454?book_show_action=true">Sep 18, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="K" class="user" itemprop="url" name="K" href="/user/show/16359109-k">K</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16359109-k?shelf=heart-wrenching">heart-wrenching</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16359109-k?shelf=made-me-cry">made-me-cry</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16359109-k?shelf=5-stars">5-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16359109-k?shelf=dual-pov">dual-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16359109-k?shelf=messed-up-heroine">messed-up-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16359109-k?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16359109-k?shelf=book-boyfriend">book-boyfriend</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16359109-k?shelf=friends-to-lovers">friends-to-lovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16359109-k?shelf=love-the-hero">love-the-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16359109-k?shelf=dark">dark</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer722885454" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15996791388519972317"><b>✮✮✮✮✮ 5 Beautifully Damaged Stars ✮✮✮✮✮</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380437105i/883930.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"She stares out the window as the late afternoon sun tries to make it's way through the window. Those gauzy curtains would make it almost impossible for her to see what’s going on inside her house, if she were ever standing on the lawn or the sidewalk looking in. But that never happens. She never leaves the house. Not even at night. Well, once she did. But then never again. The aftermath was not worth the brief taste of freedom."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br/><i>Don't Make Me Be</i></span>
  <span id="freeText15996791388519972317" style="display:none"><b>✮✮✮✮✮ 5 Beautifully Damaged Stars ✮✮✮✮✮</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380437105i/883930.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"She stares out the window as the late afternoon sun tries to make it's way through the window. Those gauzy curtains would make it almost impossible for her to see what’s going on inside her house, if she were ever standing on the lawn or the sidewalk looking in. But that never happens. She never leaves the house. Not even at night. Well, once she did. But then never again. The aftermath was not worth the brief taste of freedom."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><i>Don't Make Me Beautiful</i> by Elle Casey was <b>beautiful, touching, inspiring, heart-breaking, motivational, romantic,</b> and everything else that you could possible want in a book. It has a wonderful message about inner beauty and the strength of survival as well as the healing powers of love. This book touched my heart and it will stay with me for a long time to come. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"There would be no happy ending to this little story. She's not foolish enough to even dream otherwise. Life will never be a fairtale for a girl like her." </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><u>
  <b>Nicole</b>
</u><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"<br>No one knew a woman lived there or that she even existed. A monster, living in darkness..."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br>She's just 25 years old, but hasn't stepped foot outside in almost 3 years. She doesn't even look human anymore. Her face is so terribly disfigured from having the bones in her face broken repeatedly by The Monster. Nicole feels that her life is over, she has no hope and she wants to die. Is waiting for death to set her free. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380437105ra/883931.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"She could see one of the neighbor’s pools<br>out the back window. It was such a bright azure, so inviting. She dreamed of going over and<br>drowning herself in it many times, but then she’d look down at Kitten’s spot in the yard and know that<br>she couldn't. Then she’d be leaving Kitten behind and that never seemed right."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Then her world is irrevocably changed forever when her "superhero" <b>
  <i>Brian Jensen's</i>
</b> baseball breaks her window and forever changes her life as she knew it by culminating events that ultimately bring them together. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380437105i/883932.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Brian</b>, oh how I loved Brian! He truly is the perfect guy. Perfect in every way because Nicole needed that and I was so happy that she found that guy for her. He stood by her through thick and thin, and I couldn't adore him more for it! <i>Brian</i> is a single dad who is raising his son with the help of his ex-wife whom he is still best friends with. Brian is a goofy and sweet guy who would love to meet the right person to spend the rest of his life with. I loved how sweet Brian was with Nicole. He was sweet but he still knew how to rile her up and bring out her inner tough girl that's been waiting to come out. I loved that side of their relationship. <br> <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"You're my heart, babe. My heart. Without you I don't know what I'd do."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><i>Don't Make Me Beautiful</i> is such an inspiring story. When I closed the book I almost felt guilty for all the times that I complained about things. It made me realize how lucky most of us are and how bad some people have it. This story is probably right now someone's life, and that breaks my heart. I hope wherever she is, she finds her Brian..<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380437105i/883933._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>*****I would recommend this novel to others*****</i>
</b><br><b>If you or your loved one is suffering from domestic violence call this number now!</b><br>U.S. National Domestic Violence Hotline<br>1-800-799-SAFE (7233) or TTY 1-800-787-3224<br>UK Women’s Aid<br>Women’s Aid at 0808 2000 247<br>Australia Domestic Violence Helpline<br>1800RESPECT at 1800 737 732<br>International Directory of Domestic Violence Agencies<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.hotpeachpages.net/">http://www.hotpeachpages.net/</a><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="15996791388519972317" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_808598651" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/808598651" />
    <a title="SamJ ★Needs a HEA★" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3258936-samj-needs-a-hea"><img alt="SamJ ★Needs a HEA★" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1390412715p2/3258936.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/808598651?book_show_action=true">Jan 02, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="SamJ ★Needs a HEA★" class="user" itemprop="url" name="SamJ ★Needs a HEA★" href="/user/show/3258936-samj-needs-a-hea">SamJ ★Needs a HEA★</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3258936-samj-needs-a-hea?shelf=2-star-reads">2-star-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3258936-samj-needs-a-hea?shelf=genre-contemporary-romance">genre-contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3258936-samj-needs-a-hea?shelf=theme-abuse-issues">theme-abuse-issues</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3258936-samj-needs-a-hea?shelf=theme-insta-lust-or-love">theme-insta-lust-or-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3258936-samj-needs-a-hea?shelf=heroine-traumatic-tortured-sad-past">heroine-traumatic-tortured-sad-past</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3258936-samj-needs-a-hea?shelf=book-challenge-2014">book-challenge-2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3258936-samj-needs-a-hea?shelf=read-2014">read-2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3258936-samj-needs-a-hea?shelf=theme-abusive-ex">theme-abusive-ex</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3258936-samj-needs-a-hea?shelf=theme-cute-kids">theme-cute-kids</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3258936-samj-needs-a-hea?shelf=theme-saved-by-hero">theme-saved-by-hero</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer808598651" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3121108620589335011"><b>★Book Basics★ </b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>Genre</i>
</b>: - Contemporary Romance<br/><b>
  <i>Series</i>
</b>: - Stand Alone<br/><b>
  <i>Love triangle?</i>
</b> - <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[No <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br/><b>
  <i>Cheating?</i>
</b> - <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[No <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br/><b>
  <i>HEA? -</i>
</b> <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[Yes <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br/><b>
  <i>Would I read more by this author? </i>
</b>- Maybe<br/><b>
  <i>Rating </i>
</b>- 2<br/><br/><br/><b>★Review★</b><br/><br/>At first this started off well, even though I am not a fan of present tense. <br/><br/>The switching of the chapters from Brian's life to Nicole's life was done very well. Offering some relief while serving to highlight the</span>
  <span id="freeText3121108620589335011" style="display:none"><b>★Book Basics★ </b><br /><br /><b>
  <i>Genre</i>
</b>: - Contemporary Romance<br /><b>
  <i>Series</i>
</b>: - Stand Alone<br /><b>
  <i>Love triangle?</i>
</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><b>
  <i>Cheating?</i>
</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><b>
  <i>HEA? -</i>
</b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yes <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><b>
  <i>Would I read more by this author? </i>
</b>- Maybe<br /><b>
  <i>Rating </i>
</b>- 2<br /><br /><br /><b>★Review★</b><br /><br />At first this started off well, even though I am not a fan of present tense. <br /><br />The switching of the chapters from Brian's life to Nicole's life was done very well. Offering some relief while serving to highlight the awfulness of Nicole's life.<br /><br />And I liked the last couple of chapters.<br /><br />But the middle for me, was not good.<br /><br />I expected a heartbreaking, but beautiful, heart warming tale of a woman overcoming abuse and an awful past to find love again.<br /><br />Plot wise, it had the potential to be beautiful tale of strength, recovery and love.<br /><br />Execution wise - it just was not pulled off for me.<br /><br />I found myself questioning a lot of what happened and how and if that would happen in real life.<br /><br />Within a couple of weeks of Brian having found Nicole, they are "in love" and involved in a physical relationship.<br /><br />This is a woman, who has suffered years of abuse, has horrific injuries, missing damaged teeth, a nasal passage so messed up she cannot breath through it.<br /><br />Yet the author has Brian flirting with her almost straight away. He makes her a huge part of his life, brings her into his home after a matter of days, a home he shares with his young son, yet, he lives just around the corner from her abuser, and the only contact Nicole had had with anyone other than her abusive boyfriend in years, was with Brian and his son, and the very next day she is saved. And Brian thinks that her abuser is not going to be suspicious about who exactly saved her and where she could be?<br /><br />Nicole is in hospital, in ITU, with supposedly one of the worst cases of abuse the doctors have ever seen.<br /><br />Yet after a day, some woman is barging in all "ITU care is expensive, it needs to be paid for" Now, I do not claim to have a knowledge of the US health system or exactly how it works - but that is not right surely. What would they have done if Brian was not there, pretending to be her brother? Chucked her out?<br /><br />So she gets discharged, even though her injuries are pretty terrible, but she has no insurance, but apparently she can have some rehab as an outpatient (which never happens) No support is offered, no links to appropriate charities, help etc. Just off you go, you have no money.<br /><br />But off she goes with super hero Brian, a perfect specimen of a man. Who seems to have some need to be needed.<br /><br />At some point her abuser finds her, they both end up back in hospital and she is all of a sudden waiting on the DA to make a decision as to if she should be charged with a crime - "luckily" she does not get charged with a crime that could lead to jail time, but a lesser charge. Now, again, not an expert on US law, but I find it really hard to believe, given her situation and history, and given the donations flooding in for her, and the public sympathy she was getting at this point, that anyone would even think she should be charged with anything. She was being charged with being a helpless victim as far as I can see. It just seemed totally unbelievable and quite honestly just made me angry.<br /><br />The police seemingly cannot do anything, even though they were at the house along with the ambulance, when she is rescued, know full well the state she was in, who's house she was found in, but seem to be completely powerless to even find the bloke let alone question him. <br /><br />Why put that in the book, to add more drama? More suspense?<br /><br />Tbh, I just feel like the author bit off more than she could chew with this storyline. If you want to write it, you have to be able to really write it. Here I just felt detached from the 2 main characters. Brian especially, it all felt a bit too "perfect" and false, far far too quick. <br /><br />I did like the last couple of chapters, and was pleased for the HEA.<br /><br />But overall, I was not impressed. I just got the impression, given how quick it all happened and the insta love thing, that she would have fallen in love with whoever "rescued" her, and Brian just has the need to be the "hero" and save her. As if 5 years down the line, she no longer needs saving, or helped, and he is not needed in that way - then they will struggle being together.<br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="3121108620589335011" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer721151890" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer3255483136896428110"><b>*****5 Heart<s>breaking</s> warming Stars*****</b><br/><br/>There are so many words I can think to describe this masterpiece but so few to describe the whole story in a nutshell.<br/><br/>I cried, laughed, swooned, hated, sighed, etc......<br/><br/>This book touches every emotion while reading and so few authors have this ability to really make the reader <b>FEEL</b><br/><br/>Nicole is a young woman trapped in a relationship with a monster. A monster who has beaten her so bad that her face is distorted and has left her looking like a monster. It's beau</span>
  <span id="freeText3255483136896428110" style="display:none"><b>*****5 Heart<s>breaking</s> warming Stars*****</b><br /><br />There are so many words I can think to describe this masterpiece but so few to describe the whole story in a nutshell.<br /><br />I cried, laughed, swooned, hated, sighed, etc......<br /><br />This book touches every emotion while reading and so few authors have this ability to really make the reader <b>FEEL</b><br /><br />Nicole is a young woman trapped in a relationship with a monster. A monster who has beaten her so bad that her face is distorted and has left her looking like a monster. It's beautiful how the author creates an ironic "MONSTER" in both Nicole and John. Nicole may look like a monster on the outside but she is beautiful inside, while John looks beautiful on the outside but inside him lives a monster capable of horrific things. <br /><br />Nicole has lived a life of fear, abuse, and self-loathing for the past 3 years before Brian swoops in as a guardian angel to save Nicole from John and her life. Brian works on healing Nicole's physical wounds along with building up her self-worth. He sees Nicole for the angel she is in the inside and they both fall in love with each other.<br /><br />There are so many twists and turns in this book that will have you on the edge of your seat the whole time. <br /><br />After I finished this book - I was so curious as to who the woman was which the story was based on, but the author didn't disclose this. I was horrified thinking that woman deal with the same type of abuse that Nicole did.<br /><br />This is definitely a book worth reading and I will follow this author to see what other books she has and will write.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3255483136896428110" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

Really liked the idea of the story and the story started out ok, but as it went on some of the characters actions, mainly the main male character Brian's felt a bit too unrealistic . <div id="review_1353303997" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1353303997" />
    <a title="Jo" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14323468-jo"><img alt="Jo" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1434090906p2/14323468.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1353303997?book_show_action=true">Aug 03, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jo" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jo" href="/user/show/14323468-jo">Jo</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14323468-jo?shelf=gr2016">gr2016</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14323468-jo?shelf=3-stars">3-stars</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1353303997" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14418426216475725987"><p>For the last three years, Nicole has been violently abused by her boyfriend. She used to be a very beautiful girl, but after years of abuse her face has been so disfigured that she can’t leave the house. The mental and physical abuse has made it impossible for her to leave, and even if she could have found the courage to try again, her boyfriend locks her in their home when he’s not there so that there’s no way out.</p> <p>Until a little boy hits his baseball through her window, and a Knight comes to h</p></span>
  <span id="freeText14418426216475725987" style="display:none"><p>For the last three years, Nicole has been violently abused by her boyfriend. She used to be a very beautiful girl, but after years of abuse her face has been so disfigured that she can’t leave the house. The mental and physical abuse has made it impossible for her to leave, and even if she could have found the courage to try again, her boyfriend locks her in their home when he’s not there so that there’s no way out.</p> <p>Until a little boy hits his baseball through her window, and a Knight comes to her rescue. When Brian goes to the house to apologise for his son breaking the window, the man that answers the door just feels off for him. And because he is unable to let it go, trying to find out about the monster his son saw, he goes again the next day. What he finds is an unconscious women, badly beaten. And because Brian is a good guy, he makes it his mission to help Nicole escape her monster of a boyfriend. </p> <p>All the abuse Nicole has suffered just broke my heart, and it was at times very difficult to understand how much she was broken, up and to such a point that she just could not leave her abusive boyfriend, he brainwashed her in such a way that she believed that she deserved his abuse, that the secrets she kept would land her in worse trouble. It was heartbreaking to witness a strong and sweet woman reduced to such a weak state. </p> <p>I wish there really was guys like Brian in this world. Such selfless and sweet guys. But honestly he just came across as too good to be true. </p> <p>The romance felt like it happened way too fast, especially after all the abuse that Nicole suffered. </p> <p>This is a very difficult book to review. Although the book didn’t appeal to me, I applaud the author for writing about such a dark subject, the domestic violence that so many women are subjected to, their suffering at the hands of the person that is supposed to love and protect them. </p></span>
  <a data-text-id="14418426216475725987" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">

<span id="freeTextContainer10382684639179391078"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382494062i/5923246.jpg' alt=' photo a8716360-3607-4b21-9b97-d2a9c8e71755_zps123c7db9.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I'm kind of late to the party on this one... so I won't rehash what the story is about. What I'd like to focus on instead is the fact that this was a beautiful story about strength, hope, and perseverance. Nicole, suffered through years of domestic abuse. This man, has made her prisoner in mind, body, and spirit.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382494062ra/5923247.gif' alt=' photo tumblr_ml203hBUZH1r0y8j6o1_400_zps873e41ec.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Upon chance she meets her guardian angel and from there she meets people who are truly there for her and make her a part of. They make her feel somehing she's been scared to feel: hope.<br/><br/>I</span>
  <span id="freeText10382684639179391078" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382494062i/5923246.jpg" alt=" photo a8716360-3607-4b21-9b97-d2a9c8e71755_zps123c7db9.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I'm kind of late to the party on this one... so I won't rehash what the story is about.
