<div id="review_1915462174" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1915462174" />
    <a title="Sade" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16037420-sade"><img alt="Sade" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1605390492p2/16037420.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1915462174?book_show_action=true">Feb 18, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sade" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sade" href="/user/show/16037420-sade">Sade</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781939455123" href="/book/show/26839111-don-t-make-me-beautiful">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1915462174" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6768313674941493443"><p><br/><br/>This book had a nice premise and the first couple of chapters were actually promising but the whole plot went down hill so fast, it left my head spinning. <br/><br/><u><b>I cannot stress this enough, authors need to stop romanticising serious issues in books.</b></u><br/><br/>When authors write about Rape, Kidnapping, Domestic Violence, Pedophilia et al and label perpetrators of these acts "Anti-Heroes" it stresses me out, when they paint it in a romantic way, it <b>really really</b> does my head in.<br/><br/>Real Life is messy and frankly if yo</p></span>
  <span id="freeText6768313674941493443" style="display:none"><p><br><br>This book had a nice premise and the first couple of chapters were actually promising but the whole plot went down hill so fast, it left my head spinning. <br><br><u><b>I cannot stress this enough, authors need to stop romanticising serious issues in books.</b></u><br><br>When authors write about Rape, Kidnapping, Domestic Violence, Pedophilia et al and label perpetrators of these acts "Anti-Heroes" it stresses me out, when they paint it in a romantic way, it <b>really really</b> does my head in.<br><br>Real Life is messy and frankly if you're going to bring the ugly that is part of life into books, you owe it to your readers and yourself to tackle that issue with respect. If it's too much then just write normal romance books where the biggest complication is probably lack of communication.<br>How, i mean HOW can you write what i can only classify as total B.S on domestic violence? People die from this, people's lives are practically destroyed from this. and i think it's very appaling that this author decided to write a book about this very gritty issue but never really addresses domestic violence head on. So you expect me, the reader to believe that a woman who has been abused for 3 BLOODY years to the point that her face has been disfigured (this brings me to how unrealistic the book cover is but i'll talk about that later),who hasn't spoken to any human being apart from her abuser for those three years agrees to go and live with a MAN who from the descriptions has an almost similar build to her abuser??? You expect me to believe that the hospital let her go without any referrals to theraphy? you expect me to believe that all through the book she didn't completely lose her shit once?? Not once did she lose her shit living in a strange man's house? are fucking kidding me?<br>How is it even acceptable to tell someone that has gone through such gruesome abuse less than a week ago according to the timeline of the book to stop feeling sorry for herself? Brian goes to Nicole in this scene: </p><blockquote>
  <b>"Stop. Now you're just feeling sorry for yourself...you're not going to mop around here all day and night, feeling sorry for yourself. This house is a pity party free zone".</b>
</blockquote> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1454563634ra/17981526.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>How is that okay?<br><br>Then lets talk about the cover. I've come to the conclusion that whatever authors say in their book, they are the shallowest people ever. You'll read a book where the MC is supposedly disfigured and ugly but instead the book cover has a cover model that looks like he could walk the New York fashion show. Nicole is described as horribly deformed and her eyes are the only thing that has remained beautiful from her previous life, which, granted, is what can be seen from the cover. But can you really picture a horribly disfigured character from the cover? Because i sure as heck can't. Shouldn't something have shown? On the cover she just does look sad, yes, but otherwise perfect.<br><br> <b>
  <i>This book completely fails to deliver. It's like the author goes don't think about domestic violence too much, here's two people falling in insta love, think about that instead.</i>
</b><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="6768313674941493443" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer1423502984479296455"><br/>This book is worth <b>4.25 stars.</b> <br/><br/>This is <b>NOT</b> a bad rating because I immensely enjoyed reading this novel. <i>Nicole is a woman who has been abused for years. She has been prisoned and mistreated for a long time that she has given up on freedom.</i><br/><br/><b>This novel is good because: </b> <br/>♦ Reversed beauty and the beast.<br/>♦ The abuse aspect is different because at the start of the book, Nicole is still experiencing it. It's kind of different from other books where the hero/ine has experienced it in the past but are sti</span>
  <span id="freeText1423502984479296455" style="display:none"><br />This book is worth <b>4.25 stars.</b> <br /><br />This is <b>NOT</b> a bad rating because I immensely enjoyed reading this novel. <i>Nicole is a woman who has been abused for years. She has been prisoned and mistreated for a long time that she has given up on freedom.</i><br /><br /><b>This novel is good because: </b> <br />♦ Reversed beauty and the beast.<br />♦ The abuse aspect is different because at the start of the book, Nicole is still experiencing it. It's kind of different from other books where the hero/ine has experienced it in the past but are still wounded from it. <br />♦ I like the family aspect of this.<br />♦ There were some very unpredictable parts. <br />♦ I like how I was never able to understand John because his actions were not understandable. He was a typical socio. <br /><br /><br /><b>I also have found a few parts that wasn't very well done such as: </b><br />♦ The love aspect happened too quickly for me. <br />♦ There was a part where Liam <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ sees John abusing Nicole. For a six years old, it should've traumatized him, but in the book, he only cried at the start, and afterwards he completely forgotten about it.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Quick review:</b><br /><b>Novel:</b>Don't Make Me Beautiful.<br /><b>Author:</b> Elle Casey.<br /><b>Stars:</b> 4.25.<br /><b>Hero:</b> 3.<br /><b>Heroine:</b> 4.<br /><b>Level of sadness:</b>4.5 (Duh! The book is about abuse &amp; rape!)<br /><b>Level of darkness:</b> 4 (Only because I read darker books).<br /></span>

<div id="review_715532721" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/715532721" />
    <a title="Marti Honeycutt" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15420242-marti-honeycutt"><img alt="Marti Honeycutt" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1355327358p2/15420242.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/715532721?book_show_action=true">Sep 09, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Marti Honeycutt" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Marti Honeycutt" href="/user/show/15420242-marti-honeycutt">Marti Honeycutt</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer715532721" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14984147757482139167">I will start out by saying that hands down this is the best book I've ever read.....and I have read so many.....this one just blew my fav's out of the water. Here's why:<br/><br/>This book is not about one night stands.....whoring around.....dirty thoughts upon knowing each other 5 seconds.....characters drowning theirselves in meaningless sex and meaningless relationships yadayada.....this book just feels so real. A lot of times I finish my books and I feel like dang I just spent hours of my time on that</span>
  <span id="freeText14984147757482139167" style="display:none">I will start out by saying that hands down this is the best book I've ever read.....and I have read so many.....this one just blew my fav's out of the water. Here's why:<br /><br />This book is not about one night stands.....whoring around.....dirty thoughts upon knowing each other 5 seconds.....characters drowning theirselves in meaningless sex and meaningless relationships yadayada.....this book just feels so real. A lot of times I finish my books and I feel like dang I just spent hours of my time on that crap? Not with this book! I am proud to have read it! Now don't get me wrong i still love most or all of my romance books....but I am a very picky person when it comes to my romance books I want things to go a certain way lol yeah I know don't we all.....this book just went my way considering the circumstances of this story.....not only was I routing for the characters in this book but for the first time in reading a book I was very aware of the author I just kept thinking in my head from time to time.....you go girl! You wrote it right! There are all these books out there.....big time titles and stories that we all love....and when I got done reading this book I was like Elle Casey just surpasses them at least she does with this book....I am wanting to be her little reader cheerleader....I hope this book gets huge everyone should read it....those of us that read the likes of Sylvain Reynard.....Colleen Hoover....Abbi Gilnes.....S.C. Stephens....Jamie McGuire just to name a few.....we all sit around waiting for their new releases patiently....well Elle Casey just went on my top list of Authors to look for with their next story :) So anyway on to my review :)<br /><br />Heroine: Oh where to start its so difficult....I guess I'll start by saying she is as broken as one could possibly get and still be breathing. We don't get a lot of information about her background ( growing up....family etc.) but that's okay we get all the information we need to understand why she is in the situation she is in....which is absolutely horrible....a real life nightmare that probably happens so often we wouldn't be able to sleep at night if we knew how much of a reality this story truly is.....my heart just broke for her....I don't do a lot of crying over a story but this one well I shed a lot of tears for this young lady....I won't say to much about her physical or mental condition it's not really something I can put into words....it's something you need to read and feel. This Heroine actually makes me think of a Phoenix rising from the ashes and persevering.....especially with the help of our Hero :)<br /><br />Hero: Just when I think I've read a book and I go oh my best book boyfriend ever nobody will beat him....un huh....here in this book lies the best book boyfriend ever or to date anyways.....probably till Elle writes another book lol....<br />Our hero is the bomb! He is not a whore or a reformed whore lol god I love him! He is a Father.....a Ex-Husband/ Best Friend....He is a real Man! None of that I was hurt and now I'm gonna destroy myself lol Seriously he is so wonderful....He actually is an Angel....but he is not so great you think in your head nah I can't latch onto to him because he is just to wonderful....it's not like that! He is just a human being caring about another human being and looking deep inside to in our case the heroines soul.....her inner beauty.....her true self.....and wether or not people out there like him really exist it's such a good feeling to hope that maybe just maybe there is.....makes you wanna believe....<br /><br />Helen: for the first time ever I am going to include an Ex....let me tell you why....she was great almost as great as the main characters....but more importantly not just because she was a pretty cool Ex...she is just testament to how great our hero is.....read and you'll see why ;)<br />Agnes: heck for kicks and giggles I am gonna throw in the neighbor too....she is a neighbor I would be blessed to have.....her part in the book was small but meaningful.<br /><br />So...there is a little breakdown of our characters....<br /><br />I am so glad I had the opportunity to read this book.....I am a forever fan of Elle Casey.....<br /><br />I also wanna throw a little shout out to another book by this author Shine not Burn......which is equally as great! And also if the author reads this: just wanna mention Ian again :) want his story so bad!!!! Lol just had to throw that in there :)<br /><br />Happy Reading!</span>
  <a data-text-id="14984147757482139167" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_718159883" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/718159883" />
    <a title="Kirsty" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10389044-kirsty"><img alt="Kirsty" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1409522343p2/10389044.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/718159883?book_show_action=true">Sep 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kirsty" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kirsty" href="/user/show/10389044-kirsty">Kirsty</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10389044-kirsty?shelf=read-in-2015">read-in-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10389044-kirsty?shelf=favourites-2015">favourites-2015</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer718159883" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9521798220408993425">5 stars just aren't enough. And neither are my words. Nothing can give this book the amount of credit it deserves.<br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I'm no superhero."<br/>"Tell that to the girl you're rescuing."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17981514.Don_t_Make_Me_Beautiful' title='Don't Make Me Beautiful by Elle Casey' rel='nofollow noopener'>Don't Make Me Beautiful</a> broke my heart. I've had this book on my 'to-read' pile for a long time but have never really felt that in to the idea of reading it. For no reason at all other than there's always another book to read.. Well, I am so glad I finally decided to give it a go. It was <s>beautiful</s>.<br/><br/>Nicole is living</span>
  <span id="freeText9521798220408993425" style="display:none">5 stars just aren't enough. And neither are my words. Nothing can give this book the amount of credit it deserves.<br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I'm no superhero."<br />"Tell that to the girl you're rescuing."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17981514.Don_t_Make_Me_Beautiful" title="Don't Make Me Beautiful by Elle Casey" rel="nofollow noopener">Don't Make Me Beautiful</a> broke my heart. I've had this book on my 'to-read' pile for a long time but have never really felt that in to the idea of reading it. For no reason at all other than there's always another book to read.. Well, I am so glad I finally decided to give it a go. It was <s>beautiful</s>.<br /><br />Nicole is living through a nightmare of a life. Her partner beats her to a bloody pulp on a regular basis and she hasn't left her home in over three years. Her face is disfigured and she thinks of herself as nothing more than a monster. I admit I had a really hard time a) picturing Nicole and b) stomaching some of the stuff that she has had to live through. It was truly painful to imagine. And what's worse is we all know this goes on in the world, but when you read about it in such detail, it just brings it all home. It really is beyond worsd.<br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Scars are your body's way of healing, making that damaged part stronger than it ever was before the pain."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br />Her saviour comes in the form of Brian, a recently divorced single dad of one. He was perfection. Absolute perfection. He quite literally rescues Nicole, in all the ways that matter. And slowly but surely he helps to rebuild her life, giving her back the confidence she has lost along the way. All the while, falling in love with her. Their love story was one of the sweetest, most honest that I have ever read. Most people would think, Nicole herself included, how can he see past 'a monster'? Well, he does and I can totally see why. This book teaches you one hell of a lesson. Don't ever judge a person by their looks, not until you know their story and get to know the real person, the one inside. I think we could all take some advice from this book.<br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"You just keep on crying until all the sadness is gone, and I'll just keep wiping the tears away until you don't need me to anymore."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br />The writing in this book, as you can imagine, was flawless. I can't imagine what a difficult subject it is to write about, but <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5423648.Elle_Casey" title="Elle Casey" rel="nofollow noopener">Elle Casey</a> did it beautifully. I can't say enough positive things about this book. All I can say though is, if you get the chance, give this book a go. You certainly won't regret it.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9521798220408993425" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_720997543" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/720997543" />
    <a title="♥Sharon♥" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12125670-sharon"><img alt="♥Sharon♥" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1417537732p2/12125670.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/720997543?book_show_action=true">Sep 16, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="♥Sharon♥" class="user" itemprop="url" name="♥Sharon♥" href="/user/show/12125670-sharon">♥Sharon♥</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer720997543" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15807680512016866328">Don’t make me beautiful is a heart wrenching story about a young woman who has suffered unspeakable physical and mental abuse at the hands of someone she thought loved her. <br/><br/>Nicole’s story was painful to read. I can’t imagine surviving what she went through. Once beautiful, her face is now distorted because of so many beatings where the broken bones, cuts and bruises were left to heal on their own. My heart more than broke for her. It shattered into a million pieces. But as I turned the pages and</span>
  <span id="freeText15807680512016866328" style="display:none">Don’t make me beautiful is a heart wrenching story about a young woman who has suffered unspeakable physical and mental abuse at the hands of someone she thought loved her. <br /><br />Nicole’s story was painful to read. I can’t imagine surviving what she went through. Once beautiful, her face is now distorted because of so many beatings where the broken bones, cuts and bruises were left to heal on their own. My heart more than broke for her. It shattered into a million pieces. But as I turned the pages and finished each chapter, my heart was slowly put back together.<br /><br />At the beginning of the book the chapters are split between learning of Nicole’s torment and meeting Brian and Liam who turn out to be the ones to finally get her out of the hell that she has been living in. It was a hell that she wished she could have escaped but not only did she have insurmountable fear; she was harboring an exorbitant amount of heartache.<br /><br />When Brian first sees Nicole it is without question that he was going to care for her and help her heal somehow. It isn’t easy for him to make this decision because he has his young son Liam to think about. But with the support of his ex-wife Helen he finds away.<br /><br />Brian is an incredible person. He has the ability to look beyond a person’s physical appearance. He believes that beauty starts within a person’s heart and soul. Because of Brian’s actions and words Nicole learns to accept the love that he and the others are giving her. She begins to heal and becomes a stronger person.<br /><br />Their journey is not easy. There is heartache and comfort. There is suffering and happiness. There is rejection and acceptance. There is weakness and healing. <br /><br />Ellen Casey did an incredible job at writing this story. There were a few twists and turns in this book that had me on edge too. While I found it hard to put down, there were a few times that I had no choice. There were parts of this story that had me sobbing and truly feeling the heartache that everyone was going through. This story will have your emotions all over the place. <br /><br />My only negative point would be to say that there was a lot going on at that end of the book and while it did all come together it just felt a bit rushed.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="15807680512016866328" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

I think disturbing is a better adjective. <br/><br/>Elle Casey addressed a serious issue with this novel, but IMO, it wasn't done well.   <span id="freeText9222832740118252777" style="display:none">I'm struggling with what to say about this book.<br /><br />I see that it's labeled as dark, but I would disagree.     <a title="Imy♥♥" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17482364-imy"><img alt="Imy♥♥" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1530184908p2/17482364.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/722232759?book_show_action=true">Sep 17, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17482364-imy?shelf=on-my-kindle">on-my-kindle</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer722232759" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9674591538832970367"><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17981514.Don_t_Make_Me_Beautiful' title='Don't Make Me Beautiful by Elle Casey' rel='nofollow noopener'>Don't Make Me Beautiful</a> truly is one of those great stand alone novels. I laughed. I loved. I cried and got angry. This book took me by complete surprise!<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381007728i/3792673.jpg' alt=' photo 17981514.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>At twenty-two, Nicole no longer resembles the beautiful young girl she once was three years ago. Her face has been savagely disfigured after years of abuse, So she hides from the world and tries to survive living, with him. Hopeful that one day death will set her free from the beast.<br/><br/>Brian's a single father to his six year old son, Liam. Both wi</span>
  <span id="freeText9674591538832970367" style="display:none"><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17981514.Don_t_Make_Me_Beautiful" title="Don't Make Me Beautiful by Elle Casey" rel="nofollow noopener">Don't Make Me Beautiful</a> truly is one of those great stand alone novels. I laughed. I loved. I cried and got angry. This book took me by complete surprise!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381007728i/3792673.jpg" alt=" photo 17981514.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>At twenty-two, Nicole no longer resembles the beautiful young girl she once was three years ago. Her face has been savagely disfigured after years of abuse, So she hides from the world and tries to survive living, with him. Hopeful that one day death will set her free from the beast.<br><br>Brian's a single father to his six year old son, Liam. Both with a love of baseball, and the dream that one day they'll finally catch a fly-ball.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381010127ra/3805611.gif" alt=" photo 44444.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>That dream comes true.<br><br>Liam decides to 'borrow' the autographed ball from his dads dresser and it goes through the window of Nicole's prison, turning all their lives upside down.<br><br>This really opens up people's eyes to what can go on behind closed doors. As someone with a somewhat relatable past, I know this all to well. The wolf may dress in sheep's clothing, but he's still a wolf at the end of the day.<br><br><b>Nicole</b> was a survivor. She was thrown through the gates of hell and came out the other side, alive. She was a shadow of her former self, going through the motions, waiting for the time when the consequences of her departure from that life will arrive on the doorstep - but she was alive.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381011506i/3812618.jpg" alt=" photo depressed-woman.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> Brian </b> was such a goofy and loveable man! He was completely selfless with a huge heart. Most people once presented with a situation such as he was, would walk away and have. It's the sad truth. We need more people in the world like this fantastic fictional character Brian.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381011862i/3814256._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 600full-cam-gigandet.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b> Liam </b> melted my heart. He's the definition of adorable. (Enough said)<img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381012203ra/3815936.gif" alt="awww gifs photo: snl stefon awww tumblr_lglzyegvXF1qdtmwjo1_500.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>All of the characters, apart from one - Were easy to follow and love, and I completely devoured this book. I don't usually recommend books, but I think it's necessary. There is always going to be abuse, however if people accept it for what it is and not turn a blind eye - We can make a difference. It's not ok. It's disgusting. It's ugly. It's painful. Someone reaching out and helping could save a life.<br><br>Thankyou <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5423648.Elle_Casey" title="Elle Casey" rel="nofollow noopener">Elle Casey</a> for this beautifully dark book.</span>

<div id="review_722277717" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/722277717" />
    <a title="Vickie*** " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13185742-vickie"><img alt="Vickie*** " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1487697523p2/13185742.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/722277717?book_show_action=true">Sep 17, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Vickie*** " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Vickie*** " href="/user/show/13185742-vickie">Vickie*** </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13185742-vickie?shelf=amazing-heroines">amazing-heroines</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13185742-vickie?shelf=loved">loved</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13185742-vickie?shelf=you-make-my-heart-hurt">you-make-my-heart-hurt</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13185742-vickie?shelf=dual-pov">dual-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13185742-vickie?shelf=abuse">abuse</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer722277717" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5243672038237182716"><b> there's not enough stars/5 </b><br/><br/>Lately I have been really judgmental towards new books, and I was worried that I would criticize this book as well. THANK GOD THAT WAS NOT THE CASE<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380437016ra/883610.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>This is the first book ever where I cried more than once. It's such an emotional read. I am so glad that I came across this book!!<br/><br/>little beginning summary: <br/>Nicole is currently living with her abusive boyfriend. Not really one of those cliche book abusive bf, because not only was Nicole scarred on the inside, but on the outs</span>
  <span id="freeText5243672038237182716" style="display:none"><b> there's not enough stars/5 </b><br><br>Lately I have been really judgmental towards new books, and I was worried that I would criticize this book as well. THANK GOD THAT WAS NOT THE CASE<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380437016ra/883610.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>This is the first book ever where I cried more than once. It's such an emotional read. I am so glad that I came across this book!!<br><br>little beginning summary: <br>Nicole is currently living with her abusive boyfriend. Not really one of those cliche book abusive bf, because not only was Nicole scarred on the inside, but on the outside. Her face is damaged due to broken bones not moving back into place, swollen areas. It's just horrible.<br><br>Brian has a son named Liam. Liam was playing with a baseball, and it broke through the window of the house Nicole and asshole john are living in. <br>Now usually the books I read, kids are really sweet and kind and really try to help those in need. Liam's character in the beginning is real, this is what how real kids would react, and it's heart breaking.<br>Anyways when Liam sees Nicole he's scared and runs away, what makes me cry about this is that Nicole knows that she looks like a "monster" causing Liam to run away.<br>-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------<br>Now here are some of my thought (may contain spoilers)<br><br>-<b> brian </b> I am so in love with him. I wouldn't say he is an alpha male, he was protective but not like sexy possessive protective. He was patient, and able to look past Nicole's appearance for inner beauty. There's not a lot of guys out there (well not that I know of) right now, and it's just really nice to have that kind of hope.<br><br>-when reading the reviews, I was a tad bit iffy on reading about Helen, Brian's ex-wife and liam's mom.<br>No they don't have a bad relationship, in fact it's really good. <br>But when reading more about Helen I began to appreciate her presence in this book, her support for the family.<br><br>-Nicole's appearance: when she talks about her appearance in the beginning killed me. About how she talks about herself as a monster. <br>even later Brian and Liam even said she looked like one (not in front of her, but this KILLED me) the truth hurts...<u> a lot </u><br><i>
  <b>“There’s a real, live monster living there and I never want to go back there as long as I live.”-liam (keep in mind he's just a 6 year old, this is normal behavior) </b>
</i><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ the end where kitten is not actually dead. Now usually I would have thought this was too much, unrealistic. Though the scenario is a bit unrealistic, I'm really happy it was added. I really felt that Nicole really did have closure with her past. It was a beautiful scene having her reunite with her daughter. JUST amazing<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/396381.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>This book is heartbreaking, but it was also beautiful. It's a story of recovering, having closure, and dealing with demons. Brian and Nicole are perfect together. I am so happy that they were able to have each other.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380437016i/883611.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380437016i/883612.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This is not an erotica, there was probably only one sexy scene. But I am totally ok with that. I honestly feel if this was an erotica, that this would definitely be a very cliche book. Not all books need sex to make it a wonderful read!!<br><br>I am thrilled to have read this, I read Elle's other book, and am continuing to read her future projects!!</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="5243672038237182716" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_719547897" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/719547897" />
    <a title="Ⓑookish Ⓞne" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12889818-ookish-ne"><img alt="Ⓑookish Ⓞne" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1602527585p2/12889818.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/719547897?book_show_action=true">Sep 14, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ⓑookish Ⓞne" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ⓑookish Ⓞne" href="/user/show/12889818-ookish-ne">Ⓑookish Ⓞne</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12889818-ookish-ne?shelf=luv-it">luv-it</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer719547897" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5544675102562970531">You know how sometimes you just have that urge to find a read that will wrap itself around your heart and tug it? Well, I found this book, ‘Don’t Make Me Beautiful’ and as cliché as it may sound, it was, an instant connection.<br/><br/>I was up early Saturday morning eager to start reading. Having a late night out the night before, my mind was not truly ready for what I was about to encounter. The story is told in alternate point of views, between the H - Brian and the h - Nicole. <br/><br/>Okay, here goes….. I was</span>
  <span id="freeText5544675102562970531" style="display:none">You know how sometimes you just have that urge to find a read that will wrap itself around your heart and tug it? Well, I found this book, ‘Don’t Make Me Beautiful’ and as cliché as it may sound, it was, an instant connection.<br><br>I was up early Saturday morning eager to start reading. Having a late night out the night before, my mind was not truly ready for what I was about to encounter. The story is told in alternate point of views, between the H - Brian and the h - Nicole. <br><br>Okay, here goes….. I was in tears the first half of this book!!! At one time I was trying to figure out if it was close to that time of the month and I was probably just “hormonal”. Sob! sob! sob! Once I came to the part where the author is describing in vivid detail Nicole’s physical appearance from years of physical abuse, that image is what I saw, as I read through. I was in Nicole’s ‘state of mind’ feeling helpless, hopeless and living in hell! I desperately wished I could reach into my Kindle and be her friend, hold her hand, comfort her and save her from the monster she was living with. The abuse she endured tormented me as well. I had to take a breather from time to time; between my heart tightening and my uncontrollable sobbing! I was a total mess!<br><br>Oh Brian! With a “ruggedly handsome face, soft blue eyes and a muscular frame”. He may not be the usual, alpha male, billionaire, bad boy, CEO or rock star that we all swoon about. But, it was his kindness, compassion, patience and understanding that was attractive, admirable and awe-inspiring. Deep within was a genuine person who looked beyond Nicole’s imperfections, determined to protect her, guide and help her through the toughest of times. <br><br><div>
  <br>
  <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-KkAYwU-Ozf8/UjZe0lM3CZI/AAAAAAAAAWo/Any_Yra_bYY/s1600/perfection.jpg" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380436627i/882534.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</div><br>Even the secondary characters like Liam, Brian's son. His ex-wife Helen or Agnes the neighbor are all worthy of mention. Their characters and personalities were integral to the storyline.<br><br>Pain, anguish, misery, heartache were true emotions that I had felt. Sadness knowing Nicole’s story of physical, psychological and emotional abuse is not far from the truth for some women out here in the real world. <br><br>I know that Don’t Make Me Beautiful will linger in my mind and tug at my heart a little longer. Elle Casey has done a terrific job in this well written story. Most of all she has brought awareness to an issue some may not be aware is prevalent all around.<div>
  <br>
  <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-Js1eaFYmyNk/UjZek0PtSKI/AAAAAAAAAWg/hPnbHpJPuYE/s1600/stop-domestic-violence-logo.png" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380436627i/882535.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</div><br><div>
<br> </div>I gave this read 4.5 stars because of a few (very few) typos that threw me off a few times while reading. This is a standalone book. No cliffhanger and a HEA!<br><br>Favorite Book Quote: "You're a girl that fell in love with the wrong guy. You're face doesn't matter, it's your heart that is important. And if you can love a guy like that, then I know it has to be twice the size of a normal one" ~Brian<br><br>™From My Playlist: Coldplay – Fix You<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="5544675102562970531" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/721576375?book_show_action=true">Sep 16, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jill" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jill" href="/user/show/11270628-jill">Jill</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer721576375" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11576746496734460464">This book didn't waste time getting right into it. I liked how it described Nicole's "relationship" with John perfectly without being to graphic. I felt so sorry for her and I instantly wanted to see her get her HEA.<br/><br/>Brian and his son Liam were her angels. They saved her from "the monster". But some of the things Brian did I thought were kind of....rushed??? <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[ I didn't agree with him when he started kissing her as soon as she came home from the hospital. I thought it was a little cr</span></span>
  <span id="freeText11576746496734460464" style="display:none">This book didn't waste time getting right into it. I liked how it described Nicole's "relationship" with John perfectly without being to graphic. I felt so sorry for her and I instantly wanted to see her get her HEA.<br /><br />Brian and his son Liam were her angels. They saved her from "the monster". But some of the things Brian did I thought were kind of....rushed??? <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I didn't agree with him when he started kissing her as soon as she came home from the hospital. I thought it was a little creepy to do that to an abuse/rape victim! I read that and just thought, "WTF?! Seriously?! Already?!". <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I just felt Brian's character was a little over the top.<br /><br />I loved Nicole and Brian but their relationship was instant and I never really felt the "love" between them. I like a good build up and I missed having that in this book. <br /><br />The ending dragged on in my opinion. There was a twist toward the end that I didn't really see coming which is the reason I gave it 3 stars instead of 2. For me, it started off really, really good but kinda lost it's way somewhere in the middle. I'm not sorry I read it, but with the way it started I was hoping for so much more! <br /><br /></span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('ImchGucaPeHu+NkFBWcupvTRwMYuWi369wCVWb/AI4XllchyjQ40ua36AxUzCbhlirow28KFysZ7xTTf5l9H0g==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer18030266538856050878">Elle Casey, a former attorney and teacher, is a <i>NEW YORK TIMES</i> and <i>USA TODAY</i> bestselling American author who lives in France with her husband, the youngest of her three kids, and several horses, dogs, and cats. She has written more than 40 novels in less than 5 years and likes to say she offers fiction in several flavors. These flavors include romance, science fiction, urban fantasy, action advent</span>
  <span id="freeText18030266538856050878" style="display:none">Elle Casey, a former attorney and teacher, is a <i>NEW YORK TIMES</i> and <i>USA TODAY</i> bestselling American author who lives in France with her husband, the youngest of her three kids, and several horses, dogs, and cats. She has written more than 40 novels in less than 5 years and likes to say she offers fiction in several flavors.
